28	subTemplate = """
29	# Environment
30	# -----------
31	# There exist many universe:
32	# https://htcondor.readthedocs.io/en/latest/users-manual/choosing-an-htcondor-universe.html
33	universe = %(targetUniverse)s
34	
35	# Inputs/Outputs
36	# --------------
37	# Inputs: executable to submit
38	executable = %(executable)s
39	
40	# Directory that will contain the outputs
41	initialdir = %(initialDir)s
42	
43	# Outputs: stdout, stderr, log
44	output = $(Cluster).$(Process).out
45	error = $(Cluster).$(Process).err
46	log = $(Cluster).$(Process).log
47	
48	# No other files are to be transferred
49	transfer_output_files = ""
50	
51	# Transfer outputs, even if the job is failed
52	should_transfer_files = YES
53	when_to_transfer_output = ON_EXIT_OR_EVICT
54	
55	# Environment variables to pass to the job
56	environment = "DIRAC_PILOT_STAMP=$(stamp) %(environment)s"
57	
58	# Credentials
59	# -----------
60	%(useCredentials)s
61	
62	# Requirements
63	# ------------
64	request_cpus = %(processors)s
65	
66	# Exit options
67	# ------------
68	# Specify the signal sent to the job when HTCondor needs to vacate the worker node
69	kill_sig=SIGTERM
70	# By default, HTCondor marked jobs as completed regardless of its status
71	# This option allows to mark jobs as Held if they don't finish successfully
72	on_exit_hold = ExitCode =!= 0
73	# A subcode of our choice to identify who put the job on hold
74	on_exit_hold_subcode = %(holdReasonSubcode)s
75	# Jobs are then deleted from the system after N days if they are not idle or running
76	periodic_remove = (JobStatus != 1) && (JobStatus != 2) && ((time() - EnteredCurrentStatus) > (%(daysToKeepRemoteLogs)s * 24 * 3600))
77	
78	# Specific options
79	# ----------------
80	# Local vs Remote schedd
81	%(scheddOptions)s
82	# CE-specific options
83	%(extraString)s
84	
85	
86	Queue stamp in %(pilotStampList)s
87	"""

40	
41	echo "Starting inner container wrapper scripts at `date`."
42	set -ex
43	cd /tmp
44	# Install DIRAC
45	installer_name="DIRACOS-Linux-$(uname -m).sh"
46	if [[ -d /cvmfs/dirac.egi.eu/installSource/ ]]; then
47	  bash /cvmfs/dirac.egi.eu/installSource/"${installer_name}"
48	else

50	  bash "${installer_name}"
51	  rm "${installer_name}"

53	source diracos/diracosrc
54	pip install %(dirac_project)s==%(version)s
55	dirac-configure -F %(config_args)s -I
56	# Add compatibility with pilot3 where config is in pilot.cfg
57	ln -s diracos/etc/dirac.cfg pilot.cfg
58	# Run next wrapper (to start actual job)
59	bash %(next_wrapper)s
60	# Write the payload errorcode to a file for the outer scripts

62	chmod 644 retcode

64	
65	"""

77	except ImportError:

79	
80	# formatting with microsecond accuracy, (ISO-8601)
81	
82	class MicrosecondFormatter(logging.Formatter):
83	  def formatTime(self, record, datefmt=None):
84	    ct = self.converter(record.created)
85	    if datefmt:
86	        s = time.strftime(datefmt, ct)
87	    else:
88	        t = time.strftime("%%Y-%%m-%%dT%%H:%%M:%%S", ct)
89	        s = "%%s,%%06dZ" %% (t, (record.created - int(record.created)) * 1e6)
90	    return s
91	
92	# setting up the logging
93	# formatter = logging.Formatter(fmt='%%(asctime)s UTC %%(levelname)-8s %%(message)s', datefmt='%%Y-%%m-%%d %%H:%%M:%%S')
94	formatter = MicrosecondFormatter('%%(asctime)s %%(levelname)-8s [%%(name)s] %%(message)s')
95	logging.Formatter.converter = time.gmtime
96	try:
97	  screen_handler = logging.StreamHandler(stream=sys.stdout)
98	except TypeError:  # python2.6
99	  screen_handler = logging.StreamHandler(strm=sys.stdout)
100	screen_handler.setFormatter(formatter)
101	
102	# add a string buffer handler
103	sio = StringIO()
104	buffer = logging.StreamHandler(sio)
105	buffer.setFormatter(formatter)
106	
107	logger = logging.getLogger('pilotLogger')
108	logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
109	logger.addHandler(screen_handler)
110	logger.addHandler(buffer)
111	
112	# just logging the environment as first thing
113	logger.debug('===========================================================')
114	logger.debug('Environment of execution host\\n')
115	# Clear any non-UTF encodable environment variables as they cause the pilot to fail
116	# Use os.environb if it exists (gives raw bytes), else fall back to os.environ.
117	environb = getattr(os, "environb", os.environ)
118	for key, val in environb.items():
119	    try:
120	        # Decode if these are bytes; if they're already text, leave them as-is.
121	        if isinstance(key, bytes):
122	            key_decoded = key.decode("utf-8")
123	        else:
124	            key_decoded = key
125	        if isinstance(val, bytes):
126	            val_decoded = val.decode("utf-8")
127	        else:
128	            val_decoded = val
129	    except UnicodeDecodeError as e:
130	        logger.error("Dropping %%s=%%s due to decode error: %%s", key, val, e)
131	        del environb[key]
132	        continue
133	
134	    logger.debug(key_decoded + '=' + val_decoded)
135	logger.debug('===========================================================\\n')

137	logger.debug(sys.version)
